== '__main__':\n        FnToCLI(my_func).run()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, fn: typing.Callable):\n        self.fn = fn\n        arg_names = fn.__code__.co_varnames[: self.parser.add_argument(cli_name, **arg_opts)\n\n    def parse_args(self, args: typing.Sequence[str] | None = None):\n        self.args = self.parser.parse_args(args)\n        return self.args\n\n
